       公司產品（僅供參考）


       ANDROID SMART E-PAYMENT SOLUTIONS

       安卓智能電子支付解決方案
       General features: Powered by Android operating system and PCI PTS certified. Compact, portable, equipped with a large
                   high resolution touch screen and inbuilt camera. Support various kinds of payment options, including
                   bank card payments, Near Field Communication (“NFC”) contactless and QR code payments.
                                    PCI PTS
       一般特點：       以安卓作業系統操作，並獲得        認証。外型小巧，方便手持，具有特大高清觸控屏及內置攝像
                                          NFC
                   頭。支援各種支付方式，包括銀行卡支付、       非觸式及二維碼支付等。

       UNATTENDED SOLUTIONS

       自助服務解決方案
       General features: Ideal for self-service sales points such as railway stations, petrol stations, parking lots and kiosks.
                   Products are certified with PCI PTS and have met required standards for anti-vandalism and
                   waterproofing. Support various kinds of payment options and connectivity options include 3G, 4G, WiFi
                   and Bluetooth.

       Non-GAAP measures
                                                非公認會計原則指標
       Certain non-GAAP (generally accepted accounting principles) measures are
       used for assessing the Group’s performance. These non-GAAP measures are 若干非公認會計原則指標乃用於評估本集團的表
                                                現。但該等非公認會計原則指標並非香港公認會計
       not expressly permitted measures under GAAP in Hong Kong and may not be
                                                原則所明確認可的指標，故未必可與其他公司的同
       comparable to similarly titled measures for other companies. Accordingly, such
                                                類指標作比較，因此，該等非公認會計原則指標不
       non-GAAP measures should not be considered as an alternative to operating
                                                應視作經營收入（作為本集團業務表現指標）的替補
       income as an indicator of the operating performance of the Group or as an
                                                或經營活動現金流量（作為衡量流動資金）的替補。
       alternative to cash flows from operating activities as a measure of liquidity.
                                                提供非公認會計原則指標純綷為加強對本集團現時
       The use of non-GAAP measures is provided solely to enhance the overall
                                                財務表現的整體理解，此外由於本集團以往曾向投
       understanding of the Group current financial performance. Additionally because
                                                資者報告若干採用非公認會計原則計算的業績，因
       the Group has historically reported certain non-GAAP results to investors, the
                                                此本集團認為包括非公認會計原則指標可為本集團
       Group considers the inclusion of non-GAAP measures provides consistency in our

       The Remuneration Committee was established by the Board on 1

                                                職權範圍根據企業管治守則草擬及採納，主要

       or removal. The Remuneration Committee is also responsible for

       remuneration policy and structure to ensure that no Director or any of

       where the supplier is acting in the course of a business, if the time

      89     PAX GLOBAL TECHNOLOGY LIMITED ANNUAL REPORT 2024






       Notes to the Consolidated Financial Statements

       綜合財務報表附註


       1  GENERAL INFORMATION                   1
                                                   一般資料
          PAX Global Technology Limited (the “Company”) is an investment
                                                   百富環球科技有限公司（「本公司」）為一
          holding company and together with its subsidiaries (collectively
                                                   間投資控股公司，連同其附屬公司（統稱
          referred to as the “Group”) are principally engaged in the
                                                   「本集團」）主要從事開發及銷售電子支
          development and sales of electronic funds transfer point-of-sale
                                                   付銷售點（「電子支付終端」）產品、提供維
          (“E-payment Terminals”) products, provision of maintenance and
                                                   護及安裝及支付解決方案服務（統稱「電
          installation and payment solution services (collectively, referred to
                                                   子支付終端解決方案業務」）。
          as the “E-payment Terminals solutions business”).
          The Company is a limited liability company incorporated in
                                                   本公司為一間在百慕達註冊成立的
          Bermuda. The address of its registered office is Clarendon House,
                                                   有限責任公司，其註冊辦事處地址為
          2 Church Street, Hamilton HM 11, Bermuda. Clarendon House, 2 Church Street,
                                                   Hamilton HM 11, Bermuda
                                                                   。
          The Company’s shares were listed on the Main Board of The Stock
                                                   本公司的股份於二零一零年十二月二十
          Exchange of Hong Kong Limited (the “Stock Exchange”) on 20
                                                   日在香港聯合交易所有限公司（「聯交

          3.2 Capital management                   3.2
                                                      資本管理
             The Group regards its shareholders’ equity as capital. The
                                                      本集團將其股東權益視為資本。本
             Group’s objectives when managing capital are to safeguard
                                                      集團管理資本的目的為保障本集團
             the Group’s ability to continue as a going concern in order
                                                      能繼續以持續經營方式為股東提供
             to provide returns for shareholders and benefits for other
                                                      回報以及為其他利益相關者帶來利
             stakeholders and to maintain an optimal capital structure to
                                                      益，並且維持最佳資本結構以減少
             reduce the cost of capital.
                                                      資本成本。
             In order to maintain or adjust the capital structure, the
                                                      為維持或調整資本結構，本集團可
             Group may adjust the amount of dividends paid to
                                                      調整向股東支付股息的金額、將資
             shareholders, return capital to shareholders, issue new
                                                      本退還予股東、發行新股份、回購
             shares, repurchase the Company’s shares or sell assets to
                                                      本公司股份或出售資產以減少債
             reduce debt.
                                                      務。
             The Group monitors capital on the basis of gearing ratio.
                                                      本集團基於資本負債比率監控資
             This ratio is calculated as total debt divided by total capital.
                                                      本。該比率按債務總額除以資本總
             Total debt includes borrowings of the Group. Total capital is
                                                      額計算。債務總額包括本集團的借
             calculated as equity as shown in the consolidated balance
                                                      貸。資本總額為列於綜合資產負債
             sheet plus total debt.
                                                      表的權益加上債務總額計算。
             The Group did not have any borrowings as at 31 December
                                                      本集團於二零二四年十二月三十一
             2024 and the gearing ratio is not applicable (2023: same).
                                                      日並無借貸，故資本負債比率並不
                                                      適用（二零二三年：同上）。

          3.3 Fair value estimation                3.3
                                                      公平值估計
             (i) Fair value hierarchy                 (i)
                                                         公平值層級
                The table below analyses the Group’s financial
                                                         下表分析本集團於二零二四年
                instruments carried at fair values as at 31 December
                                                         及二零二三年十二月三十一日
                2024 and 2023 by level of valuation techniques used
                                                         按計量公平值所用的估值技術
                to measure fair values. Such inputs are categorised into
                                                         層級劃分的按公平值入賬的金
                three levels within a fair value hierarchy as follows:
                                                         融工具。該等輸入數據歸類為
                                                         公平值層級內的三個層級如
                                                         下：
                    Quoted prices (unadjusted) in active markets for
                ·                                        ·   相同資產或負債的活躍
                    identical assets or liabilities (level 1).
                                                             市場報價（未經調整）（第
                                                             一級）。
                    Inputs other than quoted prices included
                ·                                        ·   除包含於第一級的報價
                    within level 1 that are observable for the asset
                                                             外，資產或負債的可觀
                    or liability, either directly (that is, as prices) or
                                                             察直接（即價格）或間接
                    indirectly (that is, derived from prices) (level 2).

          The Group has determined the operating segments based on the

          to make strategic decisions. The Group is principally engaged in
                                                   從事電子支付終端解決方案業務及認為
          the E-payment Terminals solutions business and considers that it
                                                   其經營單一業務分類。
          operates in one single business segment.
          The chief operating decision maker assesses the performance of
                                                   主要經營決策者從地域角度按產生收入
          the Group from a geographic perspective based on the locations
                                                   之附屬公司的位置評估本集團的表現及
          of the subsidiaries in which revenues are generated and the
                                                   根據分類經營溢利╱（虧損）的計量評估
          performance of the operating segments is assessed based on the
                                                   經營分類的表現。
          measurement of segmental operating profit/(loss).
          The Group primarily operates in Hong Kong, the PRC (excluding

                                                   重大會計政策

                                                   折舊率分配其成本至剩餘價值。所採用
           at their estimated depreciation rates, as follows:

           Buildings            2% - 10%                       2% - 10%
                                                   樓宇
           Leasehold improvements 20% or over lease terms,     20%
                                                   租賃物業裝修         或按租賃年期
                                 whichever is shorter
                                                                （以較短者為準）
           Office furniture and equipment 18% - 25%            18% - 25%
                                                   辦公室傢俱及設備
           Plant and equipment  9% - 33%                       9% - 33%
                                                   廠房及設備
           Motor vehicles       18% - 25%                      18% - 25%
                                                   汽車
           No provision for depreciation is made on construction in progress
                                                   在相關資產完工並且可以用作擬定用途

           for intended use.

       15 RIGHT-OF-USE ASSETS AND LEASE LIABILITIES 15
                                                   使用權資產及租賃負債
           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           (i) Right-of-use assets                 (i)
                                                      使用權資產
              Right-of-use assets are generally depreciated over the
                                                      使用權資產一般於資產可用年期
              shorter of the asset’s useful life and the lease term on
                                                      或租賃期（以較短者為準）內按直
              a straight-line basis. If the Group is reasonably certain
                                                      線法予以折舊。倘本集團合理地確
              to exercise a purchase option, the right-of-use asset is
                                                      定會行使購買選擇權，則使用權資
              depreciated over the underlying asset’s useful life.
                                                      產於相關資產的可使用年期內予
                                                      以折舊。
           (ii) Lease liabilities                  (ii)
                                                      租賃負債
              Lease liabilities include the net present value of the
                                                      租賃負債包括固定租賃付款的淨
              fixed lease payments. Lease payments to be made under
                                                      現值。根據合理地確定會行使延續
              reasonably certain extension options are also included in
                                                      選擇權的租賃的租賃付款亦會計
              the measurement of the liability.
                                                      入其負債計量之內。
              The lease payments are discounted using the interest
                                                      租賃付款採用租賃所隱含的利率
              rate implicit in the lease. If that rate cannot be readily
                                                      予以貼現。倘無法輕易地釐定該利
              determined, which is generally the case for leases in the
                                                      率（為本集團租賃的一般情況），則
              Group, the lessee’s incremental borrowing rate is used,
                                                      使用承租人的增量借貸利率，即個
              being the rate that the individual lessee would have to
                                                      別承租人在類似經濟環境中按類
              pay to borrow the funds necessary to obtain an asset of
                                                      似條款、抵押及條件借入獲得與使
              similar value to the right-of-use asset in a similar economic
                                                      用權資產具有類似價值的資產所
              environment with similar terms, security and conditions.
                                                      需的資金而必須支付的利率。
              To determine the incremental borrowing rate, the Group,
                                                      為釐定增量借款利率，本集團在可
              where possible, uses recent third-party financing received
                                                      能情況下，使用個別承租人最近獲
              by the individual lessee as a starting point, adjusted to
                                                      得的第三方融資為出發點並作出
              reflect changes in financing conditions since third party
                                                      調整，以反映自獲得第三方融資以
              financing was received and makes adjustments specific to
                                                      來融資條件的變動，及進行特定
              the lease, e.g. term, country, currency and security.
                                                      於租賃的相關調整，例如期限、國
                                                      家、貨幣及抵押。

           Material accounting policy

           At initial recognition, the Group measures a financial asset at
                                                   於初始確認時，如非按公平值計入損益

                                                   之金融資產，本集團按該金融資產之公

                                                   平值加直接歸屬於該金融資產收購之交
           of the financial asset. Transaction costs of financial assets carried
                                                   易成本計量。按公平值計入損益之金融
           at FVPL are expensed in the consolidated income statement.
                                                   資產之交易成本則於綜合收益表列作開
                                                   支。
           Changes in the fair value of financial assets at FVPL are
                                                   按公平值計入損益之金融資產的公平值
           recognised in other gains, net in the consolidated income
                                                   變動會於綜合收益表確認為其他收益淨
           statement as applicable.
                                                   額（如適用）。
           The Group subsequently measures all equity investments at fair
                                                   本集團後續按公平值計量所有權益投
           value. Where the Group’s management has elected to present
                                                   資。倘本集團管理層選擇於其他全面收
           fair value gains and losses on equity investments in other
                                                   益列報權益投資之公平值收益及虧損，
           comprehensive income, there is no subsequent reclassification
                                                   於終止確認投資後，概不會後續重新分
           of fair value gains and losses to the profit or loss following
                                                   類公平值收益及虧損至損益。當本集團
           the derecognition of the investment. Dividends from such
                                                   有權收取股息款項時，該等投資之股息
           investments continue to be recognised in profit or loss as

       21 TRADE AND BILLS RECEIVABLES AND OTHER 21
                                                   應收賬款及應收票據及按攤銷成本
          FINANCIAL ASSETS AT AMORTISED COST
                                                   列賬之其他金融資產
           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           Trade and bills receivables including retention money receivables
                                                   應收賬款及應收票據（包括應收預扣金
           are amounts due from customers for merchandise sold or
                                                   額）為於正常業務過程中就出售商品或
           services performed in the ordinary course of business. If
                                                   提供服務而應收客戶的款項。倘應收賬
           collection of trade and bills receivables is expected in one year or
                                                   款及應收票據預期於一年內（或如屬較
           less (or in the normal operating cycle of the business if longer),
                                                   長時間，則於一般業務營運週期）收回，
           they are classified as current assets. If not, they are presented as
                                                   則分類為流動資產。否則，會被呈列為
           non-current assets.

       27 TRADE PAYABLES, OTHER PAYABLES AND    27
                                                   應付賬款、其他應付賬款及應計款
          ACCRUALS
                                                   項
           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           Trade payables are obligations to pay for goods or services that
                                                   應付賬款為於正常業務過程中從供應商
           have been acquired in the ordinary course of business from
                                                   取得商品或服務中須承擔的支付義務。
           suppliers.
           Trade and other payables are presented as current liabilities
                                                   如果付款期限少於一年（或如屬較長時
           if payment is due within one year or less (or in the normal

       28 DEFERRED INCOME TAX                   28
                                                   遞延所得稅
           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           Deferred income tax is provided in full, using the liability method,
                                                   遞延所得稅乃就資產與負債的稅基及其
           on temporary differences arising between the tax bases of assets
                                                   於綜合財務報表中的賬面值兩者間產生
           and liabilities and their carrying amounts in the consolidated
                                                   的暫時性差額，並以負債法悉數進行撥
           financial statements. However, deferred tax liabilities are not
                                                   備。然而，倘遞延稅項負債產生自商譽
           recognised if they arise from the initial recognition of goodwill.
                                                   的初始確認，則不會被確認。倘遞延所
           Deferred income tax is also not accounted for if it arises from
                                                   得稅乃產生自於除業務合併外的交易中
           initial recognition of an asset or liability in a transaction other
                                                   對資產或負債的初始確認，而於交易當
           than a business combination that at the time of the transaction
                                                   時並無影響會計或應課稅溢利或虧損且
           affects neither accounting nor taxable profit or loss and does not
                                                   不產生相等金額的應課稅及可扣減的
           give rise to equal taxable and deductible temporary differences.
                                                   暫時性差額，亦不會被確認。遞延所得
           Deferred income tax is determined using tax rates (and laws)
                                                   稅乃以於報告期末已制定或實質上已制
           that have been enacted or substantially enacted at the end of
                                                   定，並預期於變現相關遞延所得稅資產
           the reporting period and are expected to apply when the related
                                                   或償還相關遞延所得稅負債時適用的稅
           deferred income tax asset is realised or the deferred income tax
                                                   率（及法例）釐定。
           liability is settled.
           Deferred tax assets are recognised only if it is probable that
                                                   遞延稅項資產只會於未來可能有應課稅
           future taxable amounts will be available to utilise those
                                                   金額可使用該等暫時性差額及虧損時方
           temporary differences and losses.
                                                   予以確認。
           Deferred tax liabilities and assets are not recognised for
                                                   當海外業務投資的賬面值及稅基產生暫
           temporary differences between the carrying amount and tax
                                                   時性差額，而本集團有能力控制暫時性
           bases of investments in foreign operations where the Group
                                                   差額撥回的時間點，且有可能不會在可
           is able to control the timing of the reversal of the temporary
                                                   見將來撥回時，遞延稅項負債及資產則
           differences and it is probable that the differences will not reverse
                                                   不會被確認。
           in the foreseeable future.

                                                   時對其施加重大影響或共同控制，則該

                                                   外，該等政策於所有所呈列年度一直貫

                                                   徹應用。本財務報表是為本集團（包括本

          36.1 Principles of consolidation and equity accounting 36.1
                                                      合併原則及權益會計法
             (i) Subsidiaries                         (i)
                                                         附屬公司
                Subsidiaries are all entities over which the Group
                                                         附屬公司指本集團對其有控制
                has control. The Group controls an entity when
                                                         權的所有實體。本集團對實體
                the Group is exposed to, or has rights to, variable
                                                         有控制權，是指本集團因參與
                returns from its involvement with the entity and has
                                                         該實體的營運而承擔其可變回
                the ability to affect those returns through its power
                                                         報的相關風險或有權享有其可
                to direct the activities of the entity. Subsidiaries are
                                                         變回報，並能夠運用其指導實
                fully consolidated from the date on which control is
                                                         體活動的權力影響上述回報。
                transferred to the Group. They are deconsolidated
                                                         附屬公司在控制權轉移至本集
                from the date that control ceases.
                                                         團當日全數合併入賬。附屬公
                                                         司在控制權終止之日起終止合
                                                         併入賬。
                The acquisition method of accounting is used to
                                                         本集團的業務合併使用收購會
                account for business combinations by the Group (refer 36.2
                                                         計法入賬（參考附註      ）。
                to Note 36.2).
                Intercompany transactions, balances and unrealised
                                                         集團內公司間交易、結餘及集
                gains on transactions between group companies are
                                                         團公司間交易的未變現收益均
                eliminated. Unrealised losses are also eliminated unless
                                                         予以對銷。未變現虧損亦會對
                the transaction provides evidence of an impairment
                                                         銷，除非該交易提供證據顯示
                of the transferred asset. Accounting policies of
                                                         所轉讓資產出現減值情況。附
                subsidiaries have been changed where necessary to
                                                         屬公司的會計政策已按需要變
                ensure consistency with the policies adopted by the
                                                         更，以確保與本集團所採納的
                Group.
                                                         政策貫徹一致。
                Non-controlling interests in the results and equity of
                                                         附屬公司業績及權益的非控股
                subsidiaries are shown separately in the consolidated
                                                         權益分別於綜合收益表、綜合

                                                         全面收益表、綜合權益變動表

          ACCOUNTING POLICIES (continued)
          36.1 Principles of consolidation and equity accounting 36.1
                                                      合併原則及權益會計法（續）
             (continued)
             (iii) Joint arrangements                 (iii)
                                                         聯合安排
                Under HKFRS 11 “Joint Arrangements”, investments        11
                                                         根據香港財務報告準則第      號
                in joint arrangements are classified as either joint
                                                         「聯合安排」，對聯合安排的
                operations or joint ventures. The classification depends
                                                         投資須分類為共同經營或合營
                on the contractual rights and obligations of each
                                                         公司，有關分類視乎各投資者
                investor, rather than the legal structure of the joint
                                                         的合同權益和義務而定，而非
                arrangement. The Group has a joint venture.
                                                         合營安排的法律結構。本集團
                                                         擁有一間合營公司。
                Interests in the joint ventures are accounted for using
                                                         於合營公司的權益於綜合資產
                the equity method (see (iv) below), after initially being
                                                         負債表按成本初始確認後使用
                recognised at cost in the consolidated balance sheet. (iv)
                                                         權益法（見下文    ）入賬。
             (iv) Equity method                       (iv)
                                                         權益會計法
                Under the equity method of accounting, the
                                                         根據權益會計法，投資初始按
                investments are initially recognised at cost and
                                                         成本確認，隨後予以調整以確
                adjusted thereafter to recognise the Group’s share of
                                                         認本集團於被投資方所佔的收
                the post-acquisition profits or losses of the investee in
                                                         購後溢利或虧損於損益中及於
                profit or loss, and the Group’s share of movements in
                                                         被投資方其他全面收益中所佔
                other comprehensive income of the investee in other
                                                         的其他全面收益變動。已收或
                comprehensive income. Dividend received or receivable
                                                         應收聯營公司及合營企業股息
                from associated companies and joint ventures are
                                                         乃確認為投資賬面值的減少。
                recognised as a reduction in the carrying amount of
                the investment.
                Where the Group’s share of losses in an equity-
                                                         當本集團所佔按權益法入賬之
                accounted investment equals or exceeds its interest in
                                                         投資的虧損等於或超過其佔實
                the entity, including any other unsecured long-term
                                                         體的權益（包括任何其他無抵
                receivables, the Group does not recognise further
                                                         押長期應收款項）時，本集團
                losses, unless it has incurred obligations or made
                                                         不再進一步確認虧損，除非本
                payments on behalf of the other entity.
                                                         集團代表其他實體承擔義務或

          36.15 Provisions                         36.15
                                                      撥備
             Provisions are recognised when the Group has a present
                                                      當本集團因過往事件承擔現有法
             legal or constructive obligation as a result of past events,
                                                      律或推定性責任，而履行責任有可
             it is probable that an outflow of resources will be required
                                                      能導致資源的流出，且金額能夠可
             to settle the obligation and the amount can be reliably
                                                      靠地估算的情況下，撥備便會被確
             estimated. Provisions are not recognised for future operating
                                                      認。未來經營虧損不會被確認為撥
             losses.
                                                      備。
             Where there are a number of similar obligations, the
                                                      倘承擔若干類似責任，於釐定履行
             likelihood that an outflow will be required in settlement
                                                      責任導致資源流出的可能性時，將
             is determined by considering the class of obligations as a
                                                      以整類責任類別作為整體予以考
             whole. A provision is recognised even if the likelihood of an
                                                      慮。即使同類責任當中任何一項導
             outflow with respect to any one item included in the same
                                                      致資源流出的可能性甚低，撥備亦
             class of obligations might be small.
                                                      會被確認。
             Provisions are measured at the present value of
                                                      撥備以管理層於報告期末為履行現
             management’s best estimate of the expenditures required
                                                      有責任所需支出的最佳估算現值計
             to settle the present obligation at the end of the reporting
                                                      量。計算此等現值使用的貼現率為
             period. The discount rate used to determine the present
                                                      能夠反映當前市場的貨幣時間價值
             value is a pre-tax rate that reflects current market
                                                      及該負債特有風險的稅前貼現率。
             assessments of the time value of money and the risks
                                                      時間流逝導致撥備金額的增幅，會
             specific to the liability. The increase in the provision due to
                                                      被確認為利息開支。
             the passage of time is recognised as interest expense.
